    <div class="dn-widget-content-container"><div class="dn-widget-content">
      <div contenteditable="false" id="60f2123c-c8a6-4e87-8b0a-9263f186ad7b_text">

<div class="elfsight-app-f31b1053-09ea-4110-acb1-c60230dfe4fc eapps-faq eapps-faq-layout-accordion eapps-faq-template-bg eapps-faq-accordion-icon-plus eapps-faq-hide-titles eapps-widget eapps-widget-show-toolbar" id="eapps-faq-3">
<div class="eapps-faq-container" style="position: relative;">
<div class="eapps-faq-inner">
<div class="eapps-faq-header" eapps-link="title">
<div class="eui-widget-title" style="display: block;">Frequently Asked Questions</div>
</div>

<div class="eapps-faq-search-bar-container eapps-faq-search-bar-container-hide"><input class="eapps-faq-search-bar-input" eapps-link="search" placeholder="Search..." type="text" /> <span class="eapps-faq-search-bar-icon" eapps-link="searchIcon"><svg height="24" viewbox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink"> <path d="M10.5 2c4.694 0 8.5 3.806 8.5 8.5 0 1.987-.681 3.814-1.823 5.261l4.53 4.532c.39.39.39 1.024 0 1.414-.39.39-1.024.39-1.414 0l-4.532-4.53C14.314 18.319 12.487 19 10.5 19 5.806 19 2 15.194 2 10.5S5.806 2 10.5 2zm0 2C6.91 4 4 6.91 4 10.5S6.91 17 10.5 17c1.77 0 3.376-.708 4.548-1.856l.045-.051c.016-.016.033-.032.05-.046C16.292 13.876 17 12.27 17 10.5 17 6.91 14.09 4 10.5 4z" id="cpl5j9m0na"></path> <g fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd" opacity=".25"> <g> <g> <g> <g transform="translate(-661 -249) translate(68 124) translate(229 112) translate(364 13)"> <mask fill="%23fff" id="mu6xtb2jnb"> <use xlink:href="%23cpl5j9m0na"></use> </mask> <use fill="%23000" fill-rule="nonzero" xlink:href="%23cpl5j9m0na"></use> <g fill="%23000" mask="url(%23mu6xtb2jnb)"> <path d="M0 0H24V24H0z"></path> </g> </g> </g> </g> </g> </g> </svg></span></div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content" eapps-link="content">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-items" eapps-link="items" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/FAQPage">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-commonitems eapps-faq-content-category">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-items" eapps-link="categoryItems">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item" itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question" eapps-link="question"><span class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question-text" itemprop="name">Can I order just one t-shirt? </span> </div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer" eapps-link="answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer" style="height: 0px;">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer-text" eapps-link="answerText" itemprop="text">You sure can! Tee Junction offers the widest range of print methods in Australia, each suitable for different designs and quantities.
<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>Our digital t-shirt printing service offers custom t-shirts with no minimum order quantity. You can order as few as one shirt, delivered Australia wide!</div>

<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>Our screen printing option is great for bulk orders. Of course, screen printing requires a setup, so it is best for larger runs, but Tee Junction offers the lowest screenprint minimums in Australia, at only 10 units (the industry norm is 25 to 50 units!).</div>

<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>Our embroidery option also has no minimum order! You only need to pay for a setup &amp; digitization fee once per design; then, you can order as few as one unit each time!</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item" itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question" eapps-link="question"><span class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question-text" itemprop="name">How much does it cost to print a t-shirt? </span> </div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer" eapps-link="answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer-text" eapps-link="answerText" itemprop="text">Tee Junction offers custom t-shirt printing from just $22.95, personalised and delivered! There are no minimum orders, but the more you buy, the more you save.
<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>With bulk orders, screen printed, you can get custom t-shirts for as little as $8. For bulk orders, please fill in our <a href="https://www.teejunction.com.au/page/bulk-quote" target="_blank">bulk quote form</a>&nbsp;for more details.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item" itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question" eapps-link="question"><span class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question-text" itemprop="name">How can I print my own t-shirts? </span> </div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer" eapps-link="answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer-text" eapps-link="answerText" itemprop="text">With Tee Junction&#39;s online t-shirt designer, you can print your own custom t-shirts in just three easy steps. First, select from a range of quality customisable blank t-shirts. Then, with this blank canvas, add your own text, photos and designs. You can then select the quantity you need, order online, and Tee Junction will have your custom t-shirt printed and shipped, FAST!</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item" itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question" eapps-link="question"><span class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question-text" itemprop="name">Can I print on the front and back of a t-shirt? </span> </div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer" eapps-link="answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer-text" eapps-link="answerText" itemprop="text">Yes! Most of our t-shirts, sweatshirts and apparel range lets you print both on the front and back of the garment.
<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>Our standard pricing includes a single side print, either the front or the back. But you are welcome to add another side of printing for a small fee, usually $5 to $10 extra per side for digitally printed t-shirts.</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item" itemprop="mainEntity" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Question">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question" eapps-link="question"><span class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-question-text" itemprop="name">Are custom t-shirts printed in Australia? </span> </div>

<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer" eapps-link="answer" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
<div class="eapps-faq-content-category-item-answer-text" eapps-link="answerText" itemprop="text">Yes, Tee Junction is a proudly Australian and operated business. All our printing happens in-house in Melbourne and is shipped Australia wide via Auspost.
<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>We&#39;re keen to keep things local, and that&#39;s why we partner with Australia&#39;s top blank companies like AS Colour.
<div>&nbsp;</div>

<div>&nbsp;</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

    function submitToNewsletter(el) {
      if (formIsBlocked($dnj('#newsletter_signup_form'))) {
        console.log("submit to newsletter not fired. already submitted");
        return false;
      };
      console.log("submit to newsletter fired");
      while(el != null && el.tagName != "FORM") {
        el = el.parentElement;  
      }
      if(el != null) {
        $dnj.ajax({
          type: "POST",
          url: "/home/email_signup",
          data: el.serialize()
        }).done(function(data, textStatus, jqXHR ) {
          log("done:" + textStatus);
          log(data);
          window.scrollTo(0,0);
          if(data.errors) {
            dnDisplayMessage('error', null, data.errors)
          } else if(data.message) {
            dnDisplayMessage('success', null, data.message)
          };
          markFormUnblocked($dnj('#newsletter_signup_form'));
        }).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown ) {
          log("fail:" + textStatus);
          log(errorThrown);
          log(jqXHR);
          window.scrollTo(0,0);
          dnDisplayMessage('error', null, "Failed to add email to Newsletter list");
          markFormUnblocked($dnj('#newsletter_signup_form'));
        });
      }
    };

  function appendCustomStyleSheets(nodeEl) {
    var sheets = document.styleSheets;
    for(var i=0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
      var sheet = sheets[i];
      if(sheet.href != null && sheet.href.trim() != "" && !sheet.href.includes("bundlev3")) {
        nodeEl.append('<link rel="stylesheet" href="' + sheet.href + '" type="text/css" media="all">\n');
      }
    }
  }
  function initPage() {
    if(typeof dnBehaviours !== 'undefined') {
      dnBehaviours.bind(null, false);
    } else {
      $dnj(document.body).addClass("dn-behaviours-bound");
    }
    $dnj.ajaxSetup({
      headers: { 'X-CSRF-Token': dnCSRFToken }
    });
    var addStylesNode = document.getElementById("deferred-styles");
    appendCustomStyleSheets(addStylesNode);
    var replacement = document.createElement("div");
    replacement.innerHTML = addStylesNode.textContent;
    document.body.appendChild(replacement)
    addStylesNode.parentElement.removeChild(addStylesNode);
    
    // 
    
    dnInitLazyLoad();
  }
</script>
